aria-labelledby="_R_2tmreqv76_--label" id="_R_2tmreqv76_" data-size="medium" aria-current="false" style="--subitem-depth:0" href="#finding-the-expiration-date-of-an-artifact"><span class="prc-ActionList-Spacer-4tR2m"></span><span class="prc-ActionList-ActionListSubContent-gKsFp" data-component="ActionList.Item--DividerContainer"><span id="_R_2tmreqv76_--label" class="prc-ActionList-ItemLabel-81ohH">Finding the expiration date of an artifact</span></span></a></li><li data-has-description="false" class="prc-ActionList-ActionListItem-So4vC Minitocs_nested__JSAov"><a class="prc-ActionList-ActionListContent-KBb8- prc-Link-Link-9ZwDx" tabindex="0" aria-labelledby="_R_35mreqv76_--label" id="_R_35mreqv76_" data-size="medium" aria-current="false" style="--subitem-depth:0" href="#artifacts-from-deleted-workflow-runs"><span class="prc-ActionList-Spacer-4tR2m"></span><span class="prc-ActionList-ActionListSubContent-gKsFp" runs</span></span></a></li></ul></nav></div><div data-container="article" style="grid-area:content" data-search="article-body"><div id="article-contents"><div class="MarkdownContent_markdownBody__v5MYy markdown-body"><h2 id="deleting-an-artifact" tabindex="-1"><a class="heading-link" href="#deleting-an-artifact">Deleting an artifact<span class="heading-link-symbol" aria-hidden="true"></span></a></h2>
<div class="ghd-alert ghd-alert-attention" data-container="alert"><p class="ghd-alert-title"><svg version="1.1" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="octicon mr-2" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p>
<p>
Once you delete an artifact, it cannot be restored.</p>
</div>
<p>Write access to the repository is required to perform these steps.</p>
<p>By default, GitHub stores build logs and artifacts for 90 days, and this retention period can be customized. For more information, see <a href="/en/repositories/managing-your-repositorys-settings-and-features/enabling-features-for-your-repository/managing-github-actions-settings-for-a-repository#configuring-the-retention-period-for-github-actions-artifacts-and-logs-in-your-repository">Managing GitHub Actions settings for a repository</a>.</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>On GitHub, navigate to the main page of the repository.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Under your repository name, click <strong><svg version="1.1" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="octicon octicon-play" aria-label="play" role="img"><path d="M8 0a8 8 0 1 1 0 16A8 8 0 0 1 8 0ZM1.5 8a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 13 0 6.5 6.5 0 0 0-13 0Zm4.879-2.773 4.264 2.559a.25.25 0 0 1 0 .428l-4.264 2.559A.25.25 0 0 1 6 10.559V5.442a.25.25 0 0 1 .379-.215Z"></path></svg> Actions</strong>.</p>
<p><picture><source srcSet="/assets/cb-12958/mw-1440/images/help/repository/actions-tab-global-nav-update.webp 1x" type="image/webp"/><img src="/assets/cb-12958/images/help/repository/actions-tab-global-nav-update.png" alt="Screenshot of the tabs for the &quot;github/docs&quot; repository. The &quot;Actions&quot; tab is highlighted with an orange outline."/></picture></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>In the left sidebar, click the workflow you want to see.</p>
<p><picture><source srcSet="/assets/cb-40551/mw-1440/images/help/actions/superlinter-workflow-sidebar.webp 2x" type="image/webp"/><img src="/assets/cb-40551/images/help/actions/superlinter-workflow-sidebar.png" alt="Screenshot of the left sidebar of the &quot;Actions&quot; tab. A workflow, &quot;CodeQL,&quot; is outlined in dark orange."/></picture></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>From the list of workflow runs, click the name of the run to see the workflow run summary.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Under <strong>Artifacts</strong>, click <svg version="1.1" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="octicon octicon-trash" aria-label="Remove artifact ARTIFACT-NAME" role="img"><path d="M11 1.75V3h2.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75ZM4.496 6.675l.66 6.6a.25.25 0 0 0 .249.225h5.19a.25.25 0 0 0 .249-.225l.66-6.6a.75.75 0 0 1 1.492.149l-.66 6.6A1.748 1.748 0 0 1 10.595 15h-5.19a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.741-1.575l-.66-6.6a.75.75 0 1 1 1.492-.15ZM6.5 1.75V3h3V1.75a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25h-2.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25Z"></path></svg> next to the artifact you want to remove.</p>
<p><picture><source srcSet="/assets/cb-14510/mw-1440/images/help/repository/actions-delete-artifact-updated.webp 2x" type="image/webp"/><img src="/assets/cb-14510/images/help/repository/actions-delete-artifact-updated.png" alt="Screenshot showing artifacts created during a workflow run. A trash can icon, used to remove an artifact, is outlined in dark orange."/></picture></p>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="setting-the-retention-period-for-an-artifact" tabindex="-1"><a class="heading-link" href="#setting-the-retention-period-for-an-artifact">Setting the retention period for an artifact<span class="heading-link-symbol" aria-hidden="true"></span></a></h2>
<p>Retention periods for artifacts and logs can be configured at the repository, organization, and enterprise level. For more information, see <a href="/en/repositories/managing-your-repositorys-settings-and-features/enabling-features-for-your-repository/managing-github-actions-settings-for-a-repository#setting-the-artifact-and-log-retention-period-for-a-repository">Managing GitHub Actions settings for a repository</a> and <a href="/en/organizations/managing-organization-settings/configuring-the-retention-period-for-github-actions-artifacts-and-logs-in-your-organization">Configuring the retention period for GitHub Actions artifacts and logs in your organization</a>.</p>
<p>You can also define a custom retention period for individual artifacts using the <code>actions/upload-artifact</code> action in a workflow. For more information, see <a href="/en/actions/tutorials/store-and-share-data#configuring-a-custom-artifact-retention-period">Store and share data with workflow artifacts</a>.</p>
<h2 id="finding-the-expiration-date-of-an-artifact" tabindex="-1"><a class="heading-link" href="#finding-the-expiration-date-of-an-artifact">Finding the expiration date of an artifact<span class="heading-link-symbol" aria-hidden="true"></span></a></h2>
<p>You can use the API to confirm the date that an artifact is scheduled to be deleted. For more information, see the <code>expires_at</code> value returned by the REST API. For more information, see <a href="/en/rest/actions/artifacts">REST API endpoints for GitHub Actions artifacts</a>.</p>
<h2 id="artifacts-from-deleted-workflow-runs" tabindex="-1"><a class="heading-link" href="#artifacts-from-deleted-workflow-runs">Artifacts from deleted workflow runs<span class="heading-link-symbol" aria-hidden="true"></span></a></h2>
<p>When a workflow run is deleted all artifacts associated with the run are also deleted from storage. You can delete a workflow run using the GitHub Actions UI, the REST API, or using the GitHub CLI, see: <a href="/en/actions/how-tos/manage-workflow-runs/delete-a-workflow-run">Deleting a workflow run</a>, <a href="/en/rest/actions/workflow-runs?apiVersion=2022-11-28#delete-a-workflow-run">Delete a workflow run</a>, or <a href="https://cli.github.com/manual/gh_run_delete">gh run delete</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div></main><footer data-container="footer"><section class="container-xl mt-lg-8 mt-6 px-3 px-md-6 no-print mx-auto"><h2 class="f3">Help and support</h2><div
